# Corpus information

The corpus consists of elf binaries extracted from firmware images. The images are partly from the following list of vendors and device classes:

| Vendor | Device | Class |
| ---- | --------- | ------ |
| Asus | BRT-AC828 | Router |
| Asus | RT-AC1200 | Router | 
| Asus | RT-AC5300 | Router | 
| Asus | RT-AC87U | Router | 
| D-Link | DIR-895L | Router | 
| D-Link | DWC-1000 | Wireless Controller | 
| D-Link | DWL-3150 | Wireless Bridge | 
| D-Link | DXS-1210-12TC | Managed Switch | 
| Edimax | SP2101W | Smart Plug | 
| Linksys | WES610N | Wireless Bridge | 
| Linksys | WHW0303B | WLAN Mesh Module | 
| Linksys | WRT1200AC | Router | 
| Linksys | WRT160N | Router | 
| Linksys | WRT1900AC | Router | 
| Linksys | WRT1900ACS | Router | 
| Linksys | WRT3200ACM | Router | 
| Linksys | WRT32X | Router | 
| Linksys | WRT54GL | Router | 
| Linksys | WRT54G-TM | Router | 
| Linksys | WUMC710 | Wireless Bridge | 
| Linksys | WVC80N | IP Camera | 
| Netgear | R8500 | Router | 
| Netgear | WAC720 | Access Point | 
| Phicomm | K1 | Router | 
| Phicomm | K1S | Router | 
| Phicomm | K2 | Router | 
| Phicomm | K2C | Router | 
| Synology | DS110j | NAS | 
| Synology | DS112 | NAS | 
| Synology | DS112j | NAS | 
| Synology | DS209 | NAS | 
| Synology | DS211+ | NAS | 
| Synology | DS211j | NAS | 
| Synology | DS212+ | NAS | 
| Synology | DS213air | NAS | 
| Synology | DS409 | NAS | 
| Synology | DS411j | NAS | 
| Synology | RS409 | NAS | 
| Tenvis | 391W | IP Camera | 
| Tenvis | 602W | IP Camera | 
| Tenvis | JPT3815W | IP Camera | 
| Tenvis | MINI319 | IP Camera | 
| Tenvis | ROBOT2 | IP Camera | 
| Tenvis | ROBOT3 | IP Camera | 
| Tenvis | TH661 | IP Camera | 
| Tenvis | TH692 | IP Camera | 
| TP-Link | HS110 | Smart Plug | 
| TP-Link | Touch P5 | Router | 

Below you can find an attribution of binaries in the corpus to their corresponding devices.

To get more information regarding the corpus, such as how to reconstruct it, contact firmware-security@fkie.fraunhofer.de
